\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\begin{DoxyVerb}Class which encapsulates common functionality between rv_discrete
and rv_continuous.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Default check for correct values on args and keywords.

Returns condition array of 1's where arguments are correct and
 0's where they are not.
\end{DoxyVerb}

 _attach_argparser_methods. This method is called in __init__ in
 subclasses, and in __setstate__

\Hypertarget{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_ac3371ff22af94bcfe9c4bfeaf62e3c17}\index{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic@{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic}!\_construct\_argparser@{\_construct\_argparser}}
\index{\_construct\_argparser@{\_construct\_argparser}!scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic@{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_construct\_argparser()}{\_construct\_argparser()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_ac3371ff22af94bcfe9c4bfeaf62e3c17} 
scipy.\+stats.\+\_\+distn\+\_\+infrastructure.\+rv\+\_\+generic.\+\_\+construct\+\_\+argparser (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{meths\+\_\+to\+\_\+inspect}{, }\item[{}]{locscale\+\_\+in}{, }\item[{}]{locscale\+\_\+out}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Construct the parser string for the shape arguments.

This method should be called in __init__ of a class for each
distribution. It creates the `_parse_arg_template` attribute that is
then used by `_attach_argparser_methods` to dynamically create and
attach the `_parse_args`, `_parse_args_stats`, `_parse_args_rvs`
methods to the instance.

If self.shapes is a non-empty string, interprets it as a
comma-separated list of shape parameters.

Otherwise inspects the call signatures of `meths_to_inspect`
and constructs the argument-parsing functions from these.
In this case also sets `shapes` and `numargs`.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{__distn__infrastructure_8py_source_l00698}{698}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{__distn__infrastructure_8py_source}{\+\_\+distn\+\_\+infrastructure.\+py}}.

\Hypertarget{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_a638dd3917afdeaf2c422c612fcd2da65}\index{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic@{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic}!\_get\_support@{\_get\_support}}
\index{\_get\_support@{\_get\_support}!scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic@{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_get\_support()}{\_get\_support()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_a638dd3917afdeaf2c422c612fcd2da65} 
scipy.\+stats.\+\_\+distn\+\_\+infrastructure.\+rv\+\_\+generic.\+\_\+get\+\_\+support (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{args}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{kwargs}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Return the support of the (unscaled, unshifted) distribution.

*Must* be overridden by distributions which have support dependent
upon the shape parameters of the distribution.  Any such override
*must not* set or change any of the class members, as these members
are shared amongst all instances of the distribution.

Parameters
----------
arg1, arg2, ... : array_like
    The shape parameter(s) for the distribution (see docstring of the
    instance object for more information).

Returns
-------
a, b : numeric (float, or int or +/-np.inf)
    end-points of the distribution's support for the specified
    shape parameters.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Penalized negative log product spacing function.
i.e., - sum (log (diff (cdf (x, theta))), axis=0) + penalty
where theta are the parameters (including loc and scale)
Follows reference [1] of scipy.stats.fit
\end{DoxyVerb}

scipy.\+stats.\+\_\+distn\+\_\+infrastructure.\+rv\+\_\+generic.\+\_\+penalized\+\_\+nnlf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{theta}{, }\item[{}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Penalized negative loglikelihood function.
i.e., - sum (log pdf(x, theta), axis=0) + penalty
where theta are the parameters (including loc and scale)
\end{DoxyVerb}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_a863f3faaafd04277fd8b0964ddbe9d5b} 
scipy.\+stats.\+\_\+distn\+\_\+infrastructure.\+rv\+\_\+generic.\+entropy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{args}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{kwds}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Differential entropy of the RV.

Parameters
----------
arg1, arg2, arg3,... : array_like
    The shape parameter(s) for the distribution (see docstring of the
    instance object for more information).
loc : array_like, optional
    Location parameter (default=0).
scale : array_like, optional  (continuous distributions only).
    Scale parameter (default=1).

Notes
-----
Entropy is defined base `e`:

>>> import numpy as np
>>> drv = rv_discrete(values=((0, 1), (0.5, 0.5)))
>>> np.allclose(drv.entropy(), np.log(2.0))
True
\end{DoxyVerb}

scipy.\+stats.\+\_\+distn\+\_\+infrastructure.\+rv\+\_\+generic.\+interval (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{confidence}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{args}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{kwds}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Confidence interval with equal areas around the median.

Parameters
----------
confidence : array_like of float
    Probability that an rv will be drawn from the returned range.
    Each value should be in the range [0, 1].
arg1, arg2, ... : array_like
    The shape parameter(s) for the distribution (see docstring of the
    instance object for more information).
loc : array_like, optional
    location parameter, Default is 0.
scale : array_like, optional
    scale parameter, Default is 1.

Returns
-------
a, b : ndarray of float
    end-points of range that contain ``100 * alpha %`` of the rv's
    possible values.

Notes
-----
This is implemented as ``ppf([p_tail, 1-p_tail])``, where
``ppf`` is the inverse cumulative distribution function and
``p_tail = (1-confidence)/2``. Suppose ``[c, d]`` is the support of a
discrete distribution; then ``ppf([0, 1]) == (c-1, d)``. Therefore,
when ``confidence=1`` and the distribution is discrete, the left end
of the interval will be beyond the support of the distribution.
For discrete distributions, the interval will limit the probability
in each tail to be less than or equal to ``p_tail`` (usually
strictly less).
\end{DoxyVerb}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{nnlf()}{nnlf()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_a96d960d322523d1ab9034e8f563ff7b0} 
scipy.\+stats.\+\_\+distn\+\_\+infrastructure.\+rv\+\_\+generic.\+nnlf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{}]{theta}{, }\item[{}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Negative loglikelihood function.
Notes
-----
This is ``-sum(log pdf(x, theta), axis=0)`` where `theta` are the
parameters (including loc and scale).
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_aa4e78d8d58ac916e1c13995aa4ee9339}\index{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic@{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic}!random\_state@{random\_state}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{random\_state()}{random\_state()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_aa4e78d8d58ac916e1c13995aa4ee9339} 
scipy.\+stats.\+\_\+distn\+\_\+infrastructure.\+rv\+\_\+generic.\+random\+\_\+state (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Get or set the generator object for generating random variates.

If `random_state` is None (or `np.random`), the
`numpy.random.RandomState` singleton is used.
If `random_state` is an int, a new ``RandomState`` instance is used,
seeded with `random_state`.
If `random_state` is already a ``Generator`` or ``RandomState``
instance, that instance is used.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_ae57b7fd6bbe4f708bbffaec45cb238e4}\index{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic@{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic}!rvs@{rvs}}
\index{rvs@{rvs}!scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic@{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rvs()}{rvs()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_ae57b7fd6bbe4f708bbffaec45cb238e4} 
scipy.\+stats.\+\_\+distn\+\_\+infrastructure.\+rv\+\_\+generic.\+rvs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{args}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{kwds}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Random variates of given type.

Parameters
----------
arg1, arg2, arg3,... : array_like
    The shape parameter(s) for the distribution (see docstring of the
    instance object for more information).
loc : array_like, optional
    Location parameter (default=0).
scale : array_like, optional
    Scale parameter (default=1).
size : int or tuple of ints, optional
    Defining number of random variates (default is 1).
random_state : {None, int, `numpy.random.Generator`,
                `numpy.random.RandomState`}, optional

    If `random_state` is None (or `np.random`), the
    `numpy.random.RandomState` singleton is used.
    If `random_state` is an int, a new ``RandomState`` instance is
    used, seeded with `random_state`.
    If `random_state` is already a ``Generator`` or ``RandomState``
    instance, that instance is used.

Returns
-------
rvs : ndarray or scalar
    Random variates of given `size`.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_a62b4bbbd70fcaf568cce6d56d584cfee}\index{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic@{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic}!stats@{stats}}
\index{stats@{stats}!scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic@{scipy.stats.\_distn\_infrastructure.rv\_generic}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{stats()}{stats()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classscipy_1_1stats_1_1__distn__infrastructure_1_1rv__generic_a62b4bbbd70fcaf568cce6d56d584cfee} 
scipy.\+stats.\+\_\+distn\+\_\+infrastructure.\+rv\+\_\+generic.\+stats (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{args}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{kwds}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Some statistics of the given RV.

Parameters
----------
arg1, arg2, arg3,... : array_like
    The shape parameter(s) for the distribution (see docstring of the
    instance object for more information)
loc : array_like, optional
    location parameter (default=0)
scale : array_like, optional (continuous RVs only)
    scale parameter (default=1)
moments : str, optional
    composed of letters ['mvsk'] defining which moments to compute:
    'm' = mean,
    'v' = variance,
    's' = (Fisher's) skew,
    'k' = (Fisher's) kurtosis.
    (default is 'mv')

Returns
-------
stats : sequence
    of requested moments.
\end{DoxyVerb}
